Open a PR\n00364| \n00365| Full guide — manifest fields, context API, lifecycle hooks, best practices: **[CONTRIBUTING.md](CONTRIBUTING.md)**\n00366| \n00367| ## Plugin SDK\n00368| \n00369| > **[@teleton-agent/sdk](https://github.com/TONresistor/teleton-agent/tree/main/packages/sdk)** — full TypeScript types, interfaces, and API reference\n00370| \n00371| The SDK gives your plugin access to TON blockchain, Telegram messaging, inline bot mode, secrets, storage, and more — without touching any internals. Export `tools` as a function to receive it:\n00372| \n00373| ```js\n00374| export const tools = (sdk) => [{ execute: async (params, context) => { /* sdk.* available here */ } }];\n00375| ```\n00376| \n00377| ### Namespaces\n00378| \n00379| | Namespace | What it does |\n00380| |-----------|-------------|\n00381| | [`sdk.ton`](#sdkton--ton-blockchain) | Wallet, balance, send TON/jettons, NFTs, payment verification, jetton analytics |\n00382| | [`sdk.ton.dex`](#sdktondex--dex-aggregator) | STON.fi + DeDust — quotes, swaps, auto-select best DEX |\n00383| | [`sdk.ton.dns`](#sdktondns--ton-domains) | .ton domain check, auctions, bids, link/unlink, ADNL site records |\n00384| | [`sdk.telegram`](#sdktelegram--telegram-messaging) | Messages, media, scheduling, moderation, polls, stars, gifts, collectibles, stories |\n00385| | [`sdk.bot`](#sdkbot--inline-bot-mode) | Inline queries, callback buttons, colored styled keyboards |\n00386| | [`sdk.db`](#sdkdb--isolated-database) | Isolated SQLite per plugin (requires `migrate()` export) |\n00387| | [`sdk.storage`](#sdkstorage--key-value-store) | Key-value store with TTL — no `migrate()` needed |\n00388| | [`sdk.secrets`](#sdksecrets--secret-management) | 3-tier resolution: ENV → secrets store → pluginConfig |\n00389| | `sdk.log` | Prefixed logger — `info()`, `warn()`, `error()`, `debug()` |\n00390| | `sdk.config` | Sanitized app config (no secrets) |\n00391| | `sdk.pluginConfig` | Plugin-specific config merged with `manifest.defaultConfig` |\n00392| \n00393| ### `sdk.ton` — TON Blockchain\n00394| \n00395| ```js\n00396| // Wallet\n00397| const address = sdk.ton.getAddress();                      // string | null\n00398| const balance = await sdk.ton.getBalance(address?);        // { balance, balanceNano } | null\n00399| const price = await sdk.ton.getPrice();                    // { usd, source, timestamp } | null\n00400| const valid = sdk.ton.validateAddress(\"EQx...\");           // boolean\n\n(File has more lines.
